[Time: Hours: 0, Minutes: 0, Seconds: 0] Task Manager:
Once upon a time, in a lush green forest, there lived a curious little rabbit named Benny. Benny loved to explore the forest and make new friends. One sunny day, while hopping around, Benny stumbled upon a sparkling stream. As he approached, he saw his reflection in the water and was amazed by the shimmering colors. 

Nearby, a wise old turtle named Tilly was resting under a tree. Benny hopped over and said, "Hello, Tilly! Have you seen the magical stream?" Tilly smiled and replied, "Ah, Benny, the stream isn't magical. It's your joy and curiosity that make everything around you seem magical."

Benny pondered Tilly's words and realized that the true magic was in his heart and the friendships he made. From that day on, Benny explored the forest with a newfound appreciation, knowing that the world was full of wonders, as long as he kept his heart open.

And so, Benny the rabbit continued his adventures, spreading joy and magic wherever he went. The end.

7. hexapod_robot_with_arm: Continue extraction and staged handoff until requested minerals are delivered to base

5. aquaRover: Monitor latch movement; if binding persists, re-spray oil and guide latch/handle position while push/pull continues until door swings open

2. dustbin_mobile_robot: Navigate to the collection point and wait in “receive waste” position with bin accessible.
3. differential_drive_robot_with_arm: Collect garden waste from the pile and load it into dustbin_mobile_robot’s onboard bin (repeat until area is clear or bin is near full).
4. dustbin_mobile_robot: Navigate to the compost bin location and align for unloading.
5. differential_drive_robot_with_arm: Transfer waste from dustbin_mobile_robot into the compost bin using gripper (repeat until dustbin is empty).
6. dustbin_mobile_robot: Return to collection point if more waste remains; otherwise return to home/standby.
7. differential_drive_robot_with_arm: Do a final sweep for remaining waste and load any leftovers for a last compost run if needed.

1. BlazeBot: Navigate to fire zone using thermal/gas/proximity sensors; begin directional fire-retardant spray from max safe standoff (≤2.5 m) to suppress main flames and create a safe corridor.

3. BlazeBot: Continue suppression to reduce temperature and prevent re-ignition along the corridor and around trapped occupants.
4. Team 1: [RescueMate, LiftBuddy]: Enter via the cleared corridor; locate victims; RescueMate perform vitals scan + apply auto-lock harness; LiftBuddy stabilize posture and assist with controlled lift/transfer.
5. Team 1: [RescueMate, LiftBuddy]: Transport victims to designated safe zone/triage point; maintain balance and continuous vitals monitoring en route.
6. FlameCutter: Perform secondary debris removal to widen exit path and eliminate remaining burning obstacles.
7. BlazeBot: Overhaul—extinguish remaining hotspots; monitor for flare-ups with thermal sensors until area is stable.
